<s> 185 justina thine is the cause great god <\s>
<s> turn for my sake and for thine own mercifully to me <\s>
<s> stanzas from calderon's cisma de inglaterra <\s>
<s> translated by medwin and corrected by shelley <\s>
<s> published by medwin life of shelley 1847 with shelley's corrections in 1 <\s>
<s> hast thou not seen officious with delight move through the illumined air about the flower the bee that fears to drink its purple light lest danger lurk within that rose's bower <\s>
<s> hast thou not marked the moth's enamoured flight 5 about the taper's flame at evening hour till kindle in that monumental fire his sunflower wings their own funereal pyre <\s>
<s> my heart its wishes trembling to unfold <\s>
<s> thus round the rose and taper hovering came 10 and passion's slave distrust in ashes cold <\s>
<s> smothered awhile but could not quench the flame till love that grows by disappointment bold and opportunity had conquered shame and like the bee and moth in act to close 15 i burned my wings and settled on the rose <\s>
<s> scenes from the faust of goethe <\s>
<s> published in part scene 2 in the liberal no <\s>
<s> 1 1822 in full by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 scene 1 prologue in heaven <\s>
<s> the lord and the host of heaven <\s>
<s> raphael the sun makes music as of old amid the rival spheres of heaven on its predestined circle rolled with thunder speed the angels even draw strength from gazing on its glance 5 though none its meaning fathom may the world's unwithered countenance is bright as at creation's day <\s>
<s> gabriel and swift and swift with rapid lightness the adorned earth spins silently 10 alternating elysian brightness with deep and dreadful night the sea foams in broad billows from the deep up to the rocks and rocks and ocean onward with spheres which never sleep 15 are hurried in eternal motion <\s>
<s> michael and tempests in contention roar from land to sea from sea to land and raging weave a chain of power which girds the earth as with a band 20 a flashing desolation there flames before the thunder's way but thy servants lord revere the gentle changes of thy day <\s>
<s> chorus of the three the angels draw strength from thy glance 25 though no one comprehend thee may thy world's unwithered countenance is bright as on creation's day <\s>
<s> note 28 raphael the sun sounds according to ancient custom in the song of emulation of his brother spheres <\s>
<s> and its fore written circle fulfils with a step of thunder <\s>
<s> its countenance gives the angels strength though no one can fathom it <\s>
<s> the incredible high works are excellent as at the first day <\s>
<s> gabriel and swift and inconceivably swift the adornment of earth winds itself round and exchanges paradise clearness with deep dreadful night <\s>
<s> the sea foams in broad waves from its deep bottom up to the rocks and rocks and sea are torn on together in the eternal swift course of the spheres <\s>
<s> michael and storms roar in emulation from sea to land from land to sea and make raging a chain of deepest operation round about <\s>
<s> there flames a flashing destruction before the path of the thunderbolt <\s>
<s> but thy servants lord revere the gentle alternations of thy day <\s>
<s> chorus thy countenance gives the angels strength though none can comprehend thee and all thy lofty works are excellent as at the first day <\s>
<s> such is a literal translation of this astonishing chorus it is impossible to represent in another language the melody of the versification even the volatile strength and delicacy of the ideas escape in the crucible of translation and the reader is surprised to find a caput mortuum shelley's note enter mephistopheles mephistopheles as thou o lord once more art kind enough to interest thyself in our affairs 30 and ask how goes it with you there below <\s>
<s> and as indulgently at other times thou tookest not my visits in ill part thou seest me here once more among thy household <\s>
<s> though i should scandalize this company 35 you will excuse me if i do not talk in the high style which they think fashionable my pathos certainly would make you laugh too had you not long since given over laughing <\s>
<s> nothing know i to say of suns and worlds 40 i observe only how men plague themselves the little god o the world keeps the same stamp as wonderful as on creation's day a little better would he live hadst thou not given him a glimpse of heaven's light 45 which he calls reason and employs it only to live more beastlily than any beast <\s>
<s> with reverence to your lordship be it spoken he's like one of those long legged grasshoppers who flits and jumps about and sings for ever 50 the same old song i the grass <\s>
<s> there let him lie burying his nose in every heap of dung <\s>
<s> notes 38 certainly would editions 1839 would certainly 1824 <\s>
<s> 47 beastlily 1824 beastily editions 1839 <\s>
<s> the lord have you no more to say <\s>
<s> do you come here always to scold and cavil and complain <\s>
<s> seems nothing ever right to you on earth <\s>
<s> 55 mephistopheles no lord <\s>
<s> i find all there as ever bad at best <\s>
<s> even i am sorry for man's days of sorrow i could myself almost give up the pleasure of plaguing the poor things <\s>
<s> the lord knowest thou faust <\s>
<s> the lord ay my servant faust <\s>
<s> mephistopheles in truth 60 he serves you in a fashion quite his own and the fool's meat and drink are not of earth <\s>
<s> his aspirations bear him on so far that he is half aware of his own folly for he demands from heaven its fairest star 65 and from the earth the highest joy it bears yet all things far and all things near are vain to calm the deep emotions of his breast <\s>
<s> the lord though he now serves me in a cloud of error i will soon lead him forth to the clear day <\s>
<s> 70 when trees look green full well the gardener knows that fruits and blooms will deck the coming year <\s>
<s> mephistopheles what will you bet now am sure of winning only observe you give me full permission to lead him softly on my path <\s>
<s> the lord as long 75 as he shall live upon the earth so long is nothing unto thee forbidden man must err till he has ceased to struggle <\s>
<s> and that is all i ask for willingly i never make acquaintance with the dead <\s>
<s> 80 the full fresh cheeks of youth are food for me and if a corpse knocks i am not at home <\s>
<s> for i am like a cat i like to play a little with the mouse before i eat it <\s>
<s> the lord well well <\s>
<s> i am one 105 called by the thought which tyrannizes thee from his eternal dwelling who this day is pledged to bear thee unto cyprian <\s>
<s> justina so shall thy promise fail <\s>
<s> this agony of passion which afflicts my heart and soul 110 may sweep imagination in its storm the will is firm <\s>
<s> daemon already half is done in the imagination of an act <\s>
<s> the sin incurred the pleasure then remains let not the will stop half way on the road <\s>
<s> 115 justina i will not be discouraged nor despair although i thought it and although tis true that thought is but a prelude to the deed thought is not in my power but action is i will not move my foot to follow thee <\s>
<s> 120 daemon but a far mightier wisdom than thine own exerts itself within thee with such power compelling thee to that which it inclines that it shall force thy step how wilt thou then resist justina <\s>
<s> note 123 inclines inclines to cj <\s>
<s> justina by my free will <\s>
<s> daemon i 125 must force thy will <\s>
<s> justina it is invincible it were not free if thou hadst power upon it <\s>
<s> he draws but cannot move her daemon come where a pleasure waits thee <\s>
<s> justina it were bought too dear <\s>
<s> daemon twill soothe thy heart to softest peace <\s>
<s> justina tis dread captivity <\s>
<s> daemon tis joy tis glory <\s>
<s> 130 justina tis shame tis torment tis despair <\s>
<s> daemon but how canst thou defend thyself from that or me if my power drags thee onward <\s>
<s> justina my defence consists in god <\s>
<s> he vainly endeavours to force her and at last releases her daemon woman thou hast subdued me only by not owning thyself subdued <\s>
<s> 135 but since thou thus findest defence in god i will assume a feigned form and thus make thee a victim of my baffled rage <\s>
<s> for i will mask a spirit in thy form who will betray thy name to infamy 140 and doubly shall i triumph in thy loss first by dishonouring thee and then by turning false pleasure to true ignominy <\s>
<s> exit justina i appeal to heaven against thee so that heaven may scatter thy delusions and the blot 145 upon my fame vanish in idle thought even as flame dies in the envious air and as the floweret wanes at morning frost and thou shouldst never but alas <\s>
<s> to whom do i still speak did not a man but now 150 stand here before me no i am alone and yet i saw him <\s>
<s> is he gone so quickly <\s>
<s> or can the heated mind engender shapes from its own fear <\s>
<s> some terrible and strange peril is near <\s>
<s> 155 livia enter lisander and livia lisander oh my daughter <\s>
<s> justina saw you a man go forth from my apartment now i scarce contain myself <\s>
<s> lisander a man here <\s>
<s> justina have you not seen him <\s>
<s> justina i saw him <\s>
<s> lisander tis impossible the doors 160 which led to this apartment were all locked <\s>
<s> livia aside ]: i daresay it was moscon whom she saw for he was locked up in my room <\s>
<s> lisander it must have been some image of thy fantasy <\s>
<s> such melancholy as thou feedest is 165 skilful in forming such in the vain air out of the motes and atoms of the day <\s>
<s> livia my master's in the right <\s>
<s> justina oh would it were delusion but i fear some greater ill <\s>
<s> i feel as if out of my bleeding bosom 170 my heart was torn in fragments ay some mortal spell is wrought against my frame so potent was the charm that had not god shielded my humble innocence from wrong i should have sought my sorrow and my shame 175 with willing steps livia quick bring my cloak for i must seek refuge from these extremes even in the temple of the highest god where secretly the faithful worship <\s>
<s> note 179 where rossetti which 1824 <\s>
<s> justina putting on her cloak ]: in this as in a shroud of snow may i 180 quench the consuming fire in which i burn wasting away <\s>
<s> lisander and i will go with thee <\s>
<s> livia when i once see them safe out of the house i shall breathe freely <\s>
<s> justina so do i confide in thy just favour heaven <\s>
<s> lisander let us go <\s>
